Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee  

Foreword  
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)  
Be those who throw themselves without reservation  
The stories woven through history until now, and the stories currently being woven, cannot all be left as they are in the new ideal world we hope for. Everything until now must be judged. No matter how much a couple claims to love each other, that love cannot remain as a standard that humanity can commemorate in the ideal world we seek. If the love between couples is like that, then the love between parents and children is the same. No matter how much parents love their children, that love cannot be left as it is because it is not eternal and pure ideal love. The love between parents and children is like that, the love between couples is like that, and the love between siblings is also like that. The love between siblings cannot be left as it is in the ideal world that humanity hopes for.  
If the most important love to humans cannot be left as it is in the ideal world we desire, then everything else goes without saying. The relationships between rich and poor, between couples, or between siblings, which can determine happiness and unhappiness for humans, cannot be left as they are in the ideal world we desire.  
October 14, 1969 (Tuesday), Jongmyo.  
* This message was given during a worship service commemorating the 19th anniversary of his release from Hungnam Prison and the 14th anniversary of his release from Seodaemun Prison, and is also recorded in <Seongho> No. 93 (December 1969).  
8   Be those who throw themselves without reservation  
If we cannot leave the current world as it is in the ideal world, then the society we live in today cannot be left as it is in the ideal world either. Furthermore, we cannot deny that the nations or the world we live in today, or any ideology or thought, cannot be left as they are in the true ideal world.  
How did this come to be? It is because humanity did not start from the original ideal of human nature centered on goodness, but rather from the standpoint of evil that opposes goodness. Because this is the family, society, nation, and world that has been formed in this way, they must be judged again under new definitions centered on absolute goodness to reveal their true nature. Therefore, we must understand that we cannot simply pass on the connections of this world to the ideal world we desire.  
When we look at it this way, we see that parents living in this realm have gathered here, husbands have gathered here, and siblings have gathered here. When viewed in relation to the Republic of Korea, you have gathered here as members of the Korean nation, and when viewed in relation to the 3 billion people of the world, you have gathered here as members of humanity. Even if we respect an individual in this context, that standard can only remain as a value that must be denied. We must reflect once again on our own position, which is in a place that must acknowledge the denial of this value.  
To establish the origin of truth  
Then what is the origin of truth that can deny such things? To solve this problem, many saints and wise men have fought throughout history, but we know that they have not completely resolved it. Figures like Confucius or Jesus, or other globally renowned saints and wise men have struggled immensely, but they could not resolve it. The people until now have failed to resolve this issue because they only looked at the good side in trying to solve it.  
Humanity's ancestors did not start from a joyful day but rather from a sorrowful day, and because they started from that sorrowful origin, we cannot resolve the sorrowful facts without going beyond that place of sorrow. Yet, despite this, they tried to find solutions elsewhere without seeking the place of that sorrow. That is why all historical events until today remain unresolved. We have unresolved difficult problems scattered everywhere.  
So what is the most problematic issue? If humanity's ancestors fell into a sorrowful place due to the fall, we must rise to a place beyond that sorrowful place. If God was saddened because humanity's ancestors fell, then to have a day when God can be joyful, we must enter a place beyond that sorrow. Otherwise, we cannot comfort God.  
From this perspective, no one has ever tried to understand God's heart. Because they started from the sorrow of this world, if one is to be a true sage, a true person who can be a model of the ideal world humanity desires, they must step on this sorrow and seek joy from a place beyond that sorrow. Only then can it be true. However, in the realm of sin, no matter how much we seek solutions following the flow of history, we must understand that victorious joy that can step on the origin of history cannot appear in our human history.  
Today, the reason our church, and I myself, have embarked on this path is because we have realized how much God loves humanity. If God is the parent of humanity, how much has He loved humanity from the position of a parent? What is the standard of that love? These are the issues. And if God, who loves so much, has been saddened, to what extent has He been saddened? This is also a problem. Today's religious people cannot even touch on such issues.  
It is certain that after humanity's ancestors fell, God was saddened, but how much sorrow did humanity's ancestors themselves feel? Because of the fall, God was saddened, and humanity's ancestors were saddened. Above, the heavens were saddened, and below, the earth had its origin of sorrow, and how to perceive the origin of sorrow in human history is an important issue.  
Therefore, in conclusion, a man who can feel sorrow beyond the origin of sorrowful history must appear on this earth. Though thousands of years of history have passed, a man who can feel the sorrow that no one in the historical process has felt must emerge. To host God, who felt sorrow greater than that of humanity's ancestors after their fall, one must be able to stand before God and feel that sorrow. Otherwise, we must clearly understand that we cannot establish a relationship between God and His sons and daughters. This is a fact we can understand even from our daily lives when we have done wrong.  
Jesus, the one who removed sorrow and introduced joy  
Then how much sorrow did humanity's ancestors, Adam and Eve, feel after the fall? When they were expelled from the Garden of Eden, the world of freedom where they could host God, how much sorrow did they feel? What kind of cries did they utter, what kind of feelings of distress did they have, and what kind of despair did they walk into the future with? And how much sorrow did God feel while watching that? Without experiencing these things, one cannot return to the heavenly kingdom. There must be a filial son who can ascend to the place of that sorrow and feel a pain greater than that of God's grieving heart, and who can comfort God. When will such a person appear on this earth?  
From this perspective, Jesus, on the cross, even though his fate was hanging by a thread and he had a great historical mission to fulfill, when he reached a state of despair because his mission was left unfinished, he felt the heart of God who was grieving, having denied his own efforts and struggles. Therefore, he said, "Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they do!" The reason Jesus could say this was not just words, but because it was indeed true.  
Through a long historical process of 4,000 years, God raised the nation of Israel, weaving a history of suffering while proclaiming a day of victory. Therefore, no matter how difficult the circumstances, the nation of Israel, which cannot be discarded, has remained as a crystallization of sorrow throughout fierce historical struggles. If God were to abandon them because they betrayed Him, then all of God's efforts in the 4,000-year restoration history would vanish in an instant. Jesus, from the position of knowing this, discovered that he could not help but love Israel, and he found himself in the position of a son who must resolve God's resentment caused by Israel's failure to love Him. That is why he could pray, "Forgive them."  
The saddest event in God's historical process was the fall of Adam and Eve. The next saddest event was Jesus' crucifixion. Even if there are thousands and tens of thousands of patriots who lament the fate of a nation that has fallen, their sorrow is merely a sorrow within the limits of their nation. They lived and died for the hope of their nation, but they did not establish a relationship with God, who is the center of historical feelings, transcending the world. Not a single person died in that way.  
In that context, only Jesus Christ could weep with a heart that was more sorrowful than Adam's sorrow, which is why he could become the Savior who can save all people, the one who could uproot the roots of sorrow in the world and introduce the world of joy. When viewed this way, there is no logical contradiction in this fact.  
You must stand in a position where you can digest the sorrowful world and experience sorrow, rather than blindly believing that you are saved by faith. To have the subjectivity to judge all evil, you must feel sorrow from a place beyond that sorrow. Otherwise, you cannot make this judgment. And as long as you cannot make this judgment, goodness cannot appear on this earth.  
From this perspective, you must understand that today our church becomes the origin of joyful history.  
How did God feel when He looked at the scene of Adam's downfall? When God called out, "Adam, Adam!" immediately after the fall, what was Adam's heart like upon hearing that voice? What was the scene like when Adam was wringing his heart and crying miserably? This is the issue. As the Lord of heaven and earth, having created Adam as the essence of all things with the highest beauty, how did God feel when He saw Adam, who was captured by the unwanted world of Satan and fell in an instant? How sorrowful must He have been?  
The ladies here may have experienced this. When a parent gives birth and raises a child, and that beloved son or daughter falls ill and is on the brink of death, what is the heart of the parent looking at that child? If the heart of a parent in the fallen world feels that way, how much more so is the heart of the original Father? What must the heart of God, who created Adam with the highest beauty, feel when He looks at the fallen Adam? This is the issue.  
Where is the man who can step on the sorrow of humanity's ancestors and comfort God by taking on God's painful sorrow? There has yet to be a saint or wise man who has come forth centered on such issues.  
Today, we must understand well. To become a child of God, you must feel a sorrow greater than that which Adam felt after the fall and shed tears greater than those he shed. You must stand in a position of deep sorrow where your heart aches and your insides twist. Thus, you must be able to shed tears filled with sorrow onto the ground while having a heartfelt plea towards heaven, repenting of historical sins and asking for forgiveness for the heart that has been unfilial before Him. Without experiencing this, you cannot participate in the world of ideal joy where God comes, beyond this world of darkness.  
That is why today, when you are pioneering these things, you must shed the greatest tears. Also, even if you face sorrow, you must bear it with content and pride that will not yield to anyone in human history. When you stand before God and on a standard that no one on this earth can deny, that is where the resolution of this sorrowful world begins. From there, a new movement of history will unfold, presenting new goodness and new heavenly connections. Until now, we humans have gone through a long historical process, but we have not been able to present such things. Only when such things are presented will a new world of hope sprout on this earth.  
Today, whether it is the Republic of Korea or any other nation, behind the history of five thousand years lies the tears of countless patriots. The cultural background that has developed into a progressive world of history today also bears the legacy of many saints and wise men. There will also be traces of the tears they shed. However, the tears they shed did not transcend the origin of sorrow.  
That is why what we want to discuss today is God's heart. We want to discuss God's heart. To understand God's heart, one must experience the sorrow caused by the fall. I must place myself in the scenes where many prophets and ancestors who followed the will on the path of restoration have come forth and failed, and experience before God from a position that transcends history.  
The place where the new heavenly people’s thought begins  
Through one’s own experience, one must become a subject that removes evil and defends goodness.
When we become conscious, we cannot deny the fact that a new history and a new ideology of the common people begin from here. That is why we are told to endure hardships from the very bottom. In the process of weaving these stories, it is essential that God is with us. 

When a child dies, in a place of lamentation, when no one can suppress their grief or provide comfort in a miserable environment, parents are bound to participate. It is not that they cannot join in, but if they know, regardless of the circumstances, it is the heart of a parent that wants to participate. 

If there is a God whose love is several times greater than that of such parents, and if He is the Father of humanity, then when someone encounters such miserable and heartbreaking facts, God will surely be present there. It means that God must always be with him on his path. When that happens, no matter what trials and pains there are, those trials and pains cannot swallow him. However, these trials and pains are indeed a condition that can lead to the perfect conclusion of patience. 

Therefore, trials and pains are not symbols of sorrow; rather, they become an absolute factor that allows me to become a light forever, determining the value of goodness and establishing a new beginning. Unless the subject individual, the subjective stage, and the ideology of the subjective world appear with the flag of victory, it will not be possible to conquer and overthrow this world of evil. 

In this sense, there were times when I pushed you hard with tears in my eyes. There were times when I had to whip you even though I clearly knew you were sighing. Why did it have to be that way? It is because you are on a destined path that must go through a principled process, and it was an inevitable strategy to break free from the environment that had been trapped in the world of misfortune until now. 

The reason we must pursue history
Today, as you gather in such a place, it is not only important to reminisce about the past history. Rather, when we think about the realities that are developing today and the good environment, it may seem unfavorable to us. 

So why do we pursue history? It is to firmly establish how much I can follow as a true member who has kicked off the origins of history up to now and presented a new origin. 

As for myself, I have always disliked the world of sin wherever I went. Even if I suffer, I am told to live truly. Rather than singing happiness and enjoying glory in a place where all humanity criticizes, it is a precious place where humanity can ask not to die but to live even with their eyes closed, and you must understand that this is the path we have been advocating and pioneering until now. 

I have a background that you cannot even imagine. It contains historical significance. I have entered the original world and experienced it, and no matter how much anyone tries to excuse that there is no God or spiritual world, I have ample empirical materials that cannot be refuted. 

Where did these materials come from? They did not come from the connections within the living environment you have been habitually living in until now. They came from the most desperate places, where tears flowed until the eyes were swollen. They came from the sincere appeals made while kneeling and lying on the ground for days. 

When you look at history centered around the principle of restoration you have learned, you must advance to a position beyond Adam. You must go beyond the position where Adam fell. You must rise above the position where Abraham made a mistake while offering sacrifices. You must surpass the cause of Moses' failure, who aimed for the return to Canaan and caused 600,000 people to become eagle food in the wilderness. You must exceed all the causes of mistakes centered around John the Baptist and Joseph's family. 

At such times, you must not be a participant in the historical sorrow who is pushed away by that sorrow, but rather become one who can rise above that sorrow and prove goodness. From this perspective, no matter how great the trials and storms that come, if one feels those trials and storms as a love that seeks to complete their infinite value, they may be pushed to the position of a loser, but they will never fail anywhere in the world. In fact, if a close person fails, they may fail, but those who are in the right position will not fail. 

We have walked this path until now. We have always developed while facing challenges. We have emerged through the environments presented by the world's humanity. Why did we have to do that? It was because we wanted to live according to the laws of justice beyond the origins of sad history. Therefore, standing on the victory standard through the connection with Adam and Eve, who became the origin of disbelief, we must be concerned about God from the thorough position of heaven. We must go to a place of sorrow greater than God's sorrow and shed tears greater than that to comfort God. This is where religion begins. 

Every time you have such a gathering, one thing you must understand is that since history started with sorrow, we must be able to carve out the past history that we must overcome. We must become those who can completely compensate for all of that sorrow and remain. When such individuals, such couples, such families, such tribes, such nations, and such worlds emerge, this is precisely what we present today as the Third Israel. 

This Third Israel is a nation resurrected from sorrow. It is not a resurrection from a place of joy but from a place of sorrow. It is different in that it has subdued Satan in the world of sorrow. I once spoke about the incident of the solvent, but doing so is a difficult task. However, I resolved to take the most difficult escape route among the thirty million people while on the run. So, 

I will walk this path until I die! I will walk this path until my pulse stops! As long as I am still breathing, I must go. 

Because I had such a steadfast belief, I went with the conviction that I would carry the thirty million people on my back, sympathizing with their suffering as refugees. That is why no matter how shaky my legs were, I could not fall. 

In this regard, there are many among our family today who are not up to par. Those who seek to succeed moderately will fail moderately. Just look at those who boast of being chaebols in today’s Republic of Korea. They will not last for several generations. However, the foundation our church has laid will not be occupied by anyone for tens of thousands of years to come. Our church has laid its foundation according to principles that do not fundamentally deviate. 

The Unification Church, which started in prison, has joy and hope
Until now, I have lived in prison, even while in prison. I have spent about four years in prison multiple times, but that prison life has not brought me sorrow. It was my unparalleled, best dojo. It was a place where I could think about whether I can truly love humanity, whether I can truly love my enemies, and whether I can share breath with a death row inmate. It was a good dojo where I could feel the resentment of this nation and passionately criticize the injustices of society. 

That is why our church started from there. From such a place, how can we maintain the personal standards that God has presented without losing them, and how can we find a fundamental reality that can overcome any difficult environment? This has been our philosophy of living for victory until now. 

Looking at Korea today, the entire thirty million people have opposed us. They are told to oppose us. However, those who oppose will flow away with the course of history. So, let them oppose as much as they want. History is based on justice; history is based on principles. Those who cannot rise above the position where I stand and cannot surpass such principled standards will fail. 

Truth can strike evil and remain, but evil cannot strike truth and remain. Even when walking along the road, if you cause even a slight inconvenience to someone, you must not ignore it. You must apologize and say, "I am sorry!" There, age, status, or knowledge must be transcended. The same applies. Even if many countries oppose our advancement in the future, whether those who oppose us are flowing with the course of history or whether they oppose us after going through trials beyond what we have walked… 

If they oppose us from a position representing the universe and standing in for God, or if they have the content and authority of such achievements, then it is understandable; otherwise, we will never fail. 

Therefore, no matter how great America is, it cannot block our path. Even if three billion people in the world are under the dominion of Satan, they cannot stop us. If they mistakenly touch us, they will rather be caught themselves. We are pioneering this path. 

There may be those who are here for the first time today, but do not think of our Unification Church as an ordinary church. There is a tremendous struggle intertwined here. However, it is not only filled with sorrowful content. There is hope and joy that can surpass sorrow, and the authority and standards that can establish that joy have been set. That is why we have been doing this work until now. Therefore, no matter how much time passes and how much the environment changes, no one can cut the thread of hope in the heart of the man speaking here. Anyone can rise above this. 

How to become a true person is the issue
The question of how to rise to the position of a true person is an issue. If we have such abilities to overcome all the evils and anxieties of society, to seek happiness with heaven and earth as our backing, and to stand in a subjective position where we can establish the standards of goodness, it will become a global issue. This is a historical and global event. In that sense, the path we are taking will become a global issue even in the latter half of the 21st century. If it does not work, I will make it work. 

This is our thought of heavenly dominion. From this perspective, when I strike young people and come out with a club and whip, intending to inflict more suffering than I have endured, who can endure this? To inherit the treasures of heaven and earth after overcoming the rough and difficult situations through such trials, there must be someone who can accept and overcome even when I strike my trials against heaven's trials. 

How many will there be who can boast of themselves as those who have established the standards of goodness based on the foundation of overcoming such trials? 

From this perspective, the standard we speak of today regarding family is of a high dimension. When one reaches this point, their bloodline connections are not an issue. The issue is not the blood ties of tribes. This is a place where non-blood relatives can have connections beyond siblings, where non-parents can be served better than parents, and where non-families can be embraced as more than families. 

That is why, no matter how extreme the social evils one faces, they must have the subjectivity to overcome and sustain themselves. When such families, such tribes, such nations, and such worlds emerge, this evil world will surely be judged before all our authority. 

The values that a public official must have
Until now, there has not been a day when tears have dried in my eyes. It is still the same. A person in public office cannot sleep comfortably. They cannot eat a meal with peace of mind. While going through such circumstances, I have heard all sorts of things, but I did not make excuses. If God had made excuses for 6,000 years, this heaven and earth would not have remained. 

Therefore, when I touch upon God's internal heart, the trials and pains we are experiencing today are too light. It is far too insufficient to come before God and make excuses. Rather, we should comfort God and bow our heads before Him, feeling ashamed of ourselves. The more we are pushed into difficult circumstances, the more we should hide ourselves and feel ashamed, yet we are trying to make excuses. 

This should not be the case. 

If someone has a heart that is broader than any saint in world history and broader than the hearts of any sovereigns ruling the current world, they will surely remain in this world. We should create such people. 

Why did I bring out the rags I wore while in prison when I came out? Because they are worth nothing even if sold. Even if given to a candy seller, they would not be worth half a stick of candy. So, after spending nearly three years, why did I give away all my silk pants and jackets and only live in that prison uniform? 

What was the need for that rag that falls apart like cotton when touched? It is because, after ten years, a century, or even several decades, it will become a treasure that cannot be bought for any amount of money. 

If there is a chopstick that Jesus used in Jerusalem, it would not be possible to buy it even if offered Britain or America. Young people who are passionate today may laugh at this, but it is more precious than gold, which is why I brought it out while overcoming difficult circumstances. To those who know nothing, it is worth less than a single piece of clothing or a coin in their wallet. 

After enduring countless hardships, the Unification Church has lost all its precious treasures. We have lost the only precious treasure we had. It cannot be bought for any amount of money. So, am I doing this to leave such things behind? No. If I have such a heart, I will hope that God will leave it behind and that future generations will leave it behind. This is because God's heart is like this, and the hearts of future generations are like this; we do this for God and for future generations. 

This is the lifestyle and value system that those in public office must have. Even if I am tortured and collapse while spitting blood, I will say, "Heaven, please do not shed tears for me because of this blood. This will become shameful blood and tears of resentment soaked in lamentation, and I do not wish for heaven to sympathize with this."
is. Therefore, even if I end up in prison, I do not stop praying. In the realm of the heart, it is necessary to do so. However, when looking at the people of the world today, it is evident that this is not the case. That is why the teacher's dimension and position are different. 

When I face difficulties, my father also faced difficulties with me. Until now, I have shed tears for the Republic of Korea as much as any patriot. I have shed tears that come from the depths of my being. I am no less than any patriot. This is something that even without the teacher's explanation, God will understand. 

In the religious field, when viewed from the perspective of Christianity, the moments when Christians prayed before facing martyrdom, while disappearing like dew, are experiences that the teacher has gone through. Dying is simple. However, it is more difficult to walk the path of death with a destiny that should not end with death. Thus, I have navigated through nearly 50 years of life, accompanied by the history of grief and sorrow. 

In this process, God has followed me from behind, and when I was sad, He was sad with me, and when I faced difficulties, He faced them with me! This fact is an inescapable burden for me. It is a burden. When will the day come when I can completely shed this burden and joyfully praise my father in contrast to it? I fight for this. 

The path of sorrow is now flowing as it should. However, we must rise above this and carry ourselves not as losers but as victors, respecting the divine connection. The father's wish is to find sons and daughters. Therefore, you must become those who are equipped with the desire for victory and crush the authority of Satan without hesitation. 

When the father reveals His authority through such sons, is it not the father's heart to praise the true worth of the son and boast of him for eternity? Moreover, how we greet a day of joy that can be achieved is the issue. I feel that I must carry this as a mission, even if it means dying and dying again. Until now, the teacher has carried this mission. 

From this perspective, you must understand that the position of those who do not know the will or those who claim to know it but do not truly understand it is on a different dimension from the position that heaven must take. 

Today, this gathering is not to elevate the teacher's name or for publicity. We must plant roots deep in the marrow that no one can touch, creating a connection that only God, with absolute content, can access 100%. There, we must create not only sorrowful aspects but also joyful aspects. Considering this, the teacher is nearing 50... 

Can I still do this even after turning 50? When I think about it, time is pressing. 

Let us hope for the will and advance toward tomorrow. When we wake up, we must repent like sinners. After eating, when we are full, we must repent. We must live this way. Even now, I think about how to dedicate my life purely to this struggle until the end while living on this earth. You must understand this. 

Those who can be such men and women will become successors of the chosen people and ancestors who can pass on the divine connection to their descendants. Such ancestors and such sons and daughters are precious. Those who are sold for a few coins and are caught up in circumstances will all perish. 

When you knock on the door of our church, you must shed the habitual religious practices of the past. You must abandon the faith based on conceptual recognition. You must recognize God with realistic content, intuitive and leading authority, and a subjective consciousness that has absolute authority applicable to any existence. You must become sons and daughters who can remain in the sorrowful aspect forever and present a new beginning in the joyful aspect. Such people are indeed the true sons and daughters of God. 

From this perspective, every time we face such a day today, we must reflect on the past and simultaneously make a new resolution to advance toward tomorrow. Therefore, even if fierce struggles unfold before our stage, with blood and tears everywhere, I hope you become those who can throw yourselves into it without hesitation. You must have the strength to look toward the will of the world and move forward toward a vigorous tomorrow. This is the true significance of our gathering today. I sincerely ask that you become such individuals. 

<Prayer> Father, whom can I blame? The grievances of the nation must come to an end, and the grievances of the world must also come to an end. When we realize that the grievances in your heart must also come to an end, we must understand that a group must emerge on this earth, vowing to take responsibility for these grievances and struggling and weeping for them. 

October 14, this day reminds us of the day when the twists of joy and sorrow had to be traversed, making us think of how pitiful the father was. The father I call father should not have been pitiful, yet when I think of the miserable circumstances of the father, I realize I must call him father while tightening my collar. I cannot count how many times I have resented being born as a fallen descendant. 

However, in the historical process of fulfilling the mission over time, I am grateful to the grace that has allowed me to experience the deep connection in the emotional realm where the father comes to me, making it undeniable that I am with the father. 

Even if our church faces trials today, let us understand that they are nothing more than dew on the grass. 

There is a substance of trial, and that substance is the father. Also, there is a substance of overcoming, and that too is the father. If there is a king of hope, that king is the father. If there is a pitiful one who has lost all face and dignity, that too is the father. 

We, who have stepped forward to become sons and daughters of that father, know that we cannot dare to call him. We must kneel, bow our heads, and feel a heart-wrenching sorrow as we cling to the father's garment. 

The life of Jesus Christ, who walked such a path, was miserable. During his three years of public ministry, he was treated as a reactionary by his people. Thus, he disappeared on the cross along with the national grievances. 

However, even amid such suffering, we know that because the father is alive, he was resurrected with the power of resurrection. Thus, even the harsh suffering of the cross could not conquer Jesus. Because the hope of that day, when he longed for a foundation of joy, still remains, we understand that he is pioneering today’s historically chaotic society. 

In this, we know that the father himself has become the raw material of the center and the leaven, directing the course of history and creating today’s Christian democratic world. 

Today, we are in a serious position where we must inherit such historical connections and carry out a cosmic legacy. Therefore, when we think of the fact that your children gathered here are in a position of the fruits of 6,000 years of history, let us understand how tense and serious this position is. 

Let us realize today that this position is more serious than any country in history that rises and falls, and let us earnestly desire to invest the utmost value, effort, and strength into solving this issue, becoming a group that is prepared to sacrifice overall if necessary. 

As we long for this day along with the sorrows of the past, let us break through the history of sorrow flowing before the father’s wish and become those who can praise the history of joy proportional to it. Today, we are not fighting for reality, but we are fighting to greet the day of joy, so I earnestly ask that you be allowed to become heavenly warriors who can remain forever. 

Thank you for protecting us throughout this year. Please protect us until we greet another year. May everything we plan centered on the second course fulfill the standards beyond what the father desires in the public realm, and may we become sons and daughters who can fulfill the responsibilities entrusted to us in a position where the father can trust us. Thus, may we remain as symbols of joy before the father and as objects of comfort, never escaping from your embrace and your connection. I earnestly ask this. 

In the remaining time, may your mercy and love be with us, and may the eternal grace of connection accompany us throughout our lives. 

Please remember the countless children of yours who cannot attend this gathering and long for it from afar, and those children scattered overseas who shed tears longing for this land of Korea. Protect those devoted children spiritually a thousandfold and ten thousandfold, and comfort them. Let them run toward the kingdom of victory, and may they dedicate everything in today’s emotional life to become pioneers of tomorrow. I earnestly ask this and pray all these things in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> We know that countless people living on this earth from the past to the present make every effort to pursue the truth. Especially we, who are living a life of faith, know well that we aspire to become true selves while admiring the One who is the true center.

Pursuing the True
True individuals, true families, true nations, true worlds—this is not something we pursue only today; it has been pursued in the past, is being pursued in the present, and will continue to be pursued in the future.

So where will the true center that emerges through the past, present, and future culminate? It will not culminate in the world, nor in any specific country, nor in any particular society. The standard of truth must culminate in individuals, and a new beginning must be made from there. Otherwise, there can be no true families, true societies, true nations, or true worlds.

Thus, who can be the being that can be the center of truth? It is each one of us. Each of us pursues our true selves, which is why we revere God, who is the center of truth. However, the center of truth must not remain only with God. Humans must become the center.

When we say that humans must be the center, we do not mean that all humans in this world must be the center in a vague sense. Each of us must stand in a position where we can manifest as the center of the world. Otherwise, we cannot become the center of truth.

No matter how true God may be, it cannot be done with God alone. Rather, it must establish a connection with the environment and relationships. The vertical God cannot establish a relationship of truth without connecting with the horizontal environment. To achieve the purpose of a concrete goal, it is essential to establish a counterpart and determine the center.

All beings and all things in heaven and earth exist centered on the duality of masculinity and femininity. The origins of failure do not lie in years but in moments. The moment a nation falls, it is a critical juncture. The decision is made in that instant. If you can identify this moment, you will become a victor. This is where the history of hope begins. 

Reflect on how you have approached the path of the providence over the years. When the universe mobilizes to welcome you, how have you responded to that calling? Have you treated it with the respect it deserves, or have you turned away? 

God has given you this singular moment, yet many have disregarded it. If you ignore this moment, you may find yourself falling away from it, descending through personal, familial, tribal, and national levels. 

If you disregard it from a high standard, you may find it returning to you from a slightly lower standard. Therefore, you must invest your sincerity to return to the former position. 

If you miss this opportunity, you will descend further. If that happens, you will need to make reparations to restore the previous standards. If these reparations accumulate, your life will become completely blocked. You may know what to do, but no matter how hard you try, it will not work because you have lost the moment. 

You must set everything aside and analyze your past life, repenting for your mistakes and stepping over the wrong connections. The struggle there is fierce. You must invest your life in this battle. Without fighting for your very existence, you cannot escape. 

You must recognize that the connections of the universe are serious, and they are calling you with the authority of life and death, without any forgiveness for even a moment. 

Two thousand years ago, how was Joseph able to welcome Jesus, and how was Mary able to conceive Him? They were the rightful owners who could embrace a historical moment. Therefore, it is essential to seize the moment well. 

When that moment comes, will it come with joy, sorrow, despair, hope, or happiness?
The question is whether it will come. The time will not come solely based on the standards of happiness. It does not come only based on the standards I like. It comes with both the standards I dislike and the aspirational standards; in other words, it comes with the dual directions of opposites. 

In short, it would be nice if it came based on the requirements of happiness, but what will you do when it appears based on the requirements of unhappiness? Most people reject this. Such a time does not come only through the content of happiness, but rather comes through the crossroads of unhappiness and death. Therefore, it is easy for humanity to miss this time. It does not come through joyful and good circumstances, but rather through sad, oppressed, and miserable places. It is inevitable. 

To leave a true life, for fallen humanity, unhappiness and happiness began at a single crossroads. However, unhappiness must appear first before happiness comes. A person who has fallen into the place of unhappiness must step on the heat of unhappiness to rise to the place of happiness. You must understand that happiness cannot be found without doing so. 

That is why the path of religion is the path of the cross. Among them, the Unification Church must walk the path of the cross both internally and externally. It must bear the cross of the nation alone and bear the cross of the world alone. You must understand that the time of happiness is coming to the place where all humanity is waving their hands and fleeing, believing that misfortune resides there. 

From this perspective, the year 1960 was a time when happiness came to the Unification Church. It was indeed a time that could determine the history of the world. That time was a precious moment that connected our Unification Church believers to happiness more than any other era. You must understand that it was a time when the environment was being surrounded for the sake of true happiness.

Therefore, in order for you to leave a true life, it is extremely important how sincere you were in each moment that can determine a true day.

Standing in such a position, when looking at the world, the teacher is at the very top. How to leave a true life 
If it tilts even slightly to one side, it cannot be. If it tilts even a little, it will fall. This is the position you must walk through life feeling such things. If you make even a small mistake in the decisions you have to make, the world will tilt. 

The important thing in building a house is to lay the foundation correctly. If you cannot lay this correctly, no matter how splendidly you build a cultural altar or a high-rise building, it will collapse all at once. The higher it is, the greater it is, the more it will be destroyed and turned upside down to the roots. 

That is why you must establish a standard of historical victory that does not lean to one side and create the foundation of life and the foundation of your life. In doing so, you must engage in a battle that is fiercer than any battle that has appeared in the historical process. The fight centered on the problems of the external world can be resolved with death, but this is a problem that cannot be resolved even with death. Therefore, you must understand that how to establish the standard of true living is the most important issue. 

When you stand before the crossroads of death and say that you can solve all those problems, that moment is truly a solemn moment. To do this, you must absorb and digest any difficulties with joy. You must not digest them with sorrow. You must continue the fight that can leave a connection of joy. The life of a person who lives for such a moment is of infinite value. We must leave such a life behind.

Then how do you establish a true standard that does not leave regrets about this land? You must put in all your sincerity. To do this, you must have a heart that can repent even after sleeping and can repent even after eating.

True living begins with a true day, and a true day begins with a true moment. Therefore, how to continue a true day like a true moment, a true year like a true moment, and a true life like a true moment is the task left for your life. 

Some people live their lives saying, "This is my life," and let their youth, which is only a moment, slip away in vain. Such a life is a common life. Even Satan dislikes such people. Therefore, it is important to determine my value that can be like that.

How are good and evil determined? 
In a time that comes only once and cannot come again, how will you draw the path of a life of infinite value and how will you settle it? When you start, you start centered on a line on a flat surface. However, when you go, you go in different directions. Your heart wants to rise in a straight line toward a good place, but your body does not go in a straight line. How do you go? Sometimes you go to this place, sometimes to that place, and sometimes you go down and sometimes you go up; all sorts of things happen. Some people go and bend and die. That is how life is lived. 

When you die, you will be weighed whether it is plus or minus. Then, depending on how much plus or minus there is, you will be divided into heaven or hell. If minus 100 comes out, you go straight to hell. Then when does it become plus? That is the question. 

When you say a word, that word is determined by whether it is an upward word or a downward word when viewed from the horizon of heaven and earth. Even the expression of a smile is all weighed. Even if you smiled without any thought, it is distinguished as a minus smile or a plus smile. What do we call a person who smiles without intention or frivolously? We say they are out of their mind, right? 

Your eyes are the same. Centered on what you see, it is weighed whether it is a plus eye or a minus eye. The same goes for your ears. Are they plus ears or minus ears? And the same goes for your heart; is it a plus heart or a minus heart? When you think about all the actions you take based on the stimulation of your five senses, it is frightening to think that those actions are divided into plus and minus. Is Satan snatching you away, or is God taking you? You cannot just believe in words. You cannot just say you love God with words. 

No matter how unfortunate a person is, if you ask them if they know they have parents, there is no one who says they do not know. Also, if you ask them if their parents worked hard for them, no one answers that they did not, because inwardly they know their parents worked hard. Everyone knows. If someone does not know that their parents worked hard for them, what kind of unfilial child would that be? Isn’t that right? No matter how much a child may be ungrateful to their parents, they know that their parents love them. They cannot forget that they are loved. They are not unaware of it. 

You know whether what you are doing is right or wrong. Even when you commit a sin, you do not fail to recognize that you are committing a sin. You know. Because you know you are committing a sin, you cannot be forgiven. In the world, if you commit a sin intentionally, you cannot be forgiven. Isn’t that so? It is different from cases where you are forced by your environment to commit a sin passively. When investigating a crime, they talk about whether someone is the main offender, an accomplice, or involved; it is about whether it is intentional or passive. 

So, is there anyone who commits unfilial acts without knowing? Does someone who sells out their country not know? Everyone knows. When you do something bad, do you not know it is bad? Do you know or not? There is not a single thing you do without knowing. 

So, whom will you make excuses to for what you did knowingly? Who will you make excuses to for what you did knowing it was wrong? You must take responsibility for yourself; there is no one to blame. You must indemnify that person for the wrong you knowingly committed. 

Even in listening to songs, there is good and evil. In seeing, hearing, eating, sleeping, and waking, everything has good and evil. In times of war, when fierce battles are taking place and everyone is going out to fight, can you just lie down and sleep? Normally, you can sleep as much as you want without feeling guilty, but if your comrades are going out to fight and you are the only one not fighting, you will feel guilty. You know it all. 

Your entire life journey will determine good and evil based on the actions you have taken. Even a single word is the same. The words the teacher is speaking now are all being judged on how many good words and how many bad words are being spoken. They are discerning between false words and true words. 

You must strive to become a life that everyone can rejoice in. 
So, what kind of being is God? God is the one who does not go down to the position of a minus standard. No matter how hard Satan tries, he cannot rise to the plus standard. However, people are in a position where they are being pulled up and down in between. 

When you look at your life, everyone is born happily. Then, as you go, you will settle how much minus and how much plus you have. Then, there should be more plus, so how can you leave more plus? You must take what you can truly say was good throughout your life as a model for your life. Do not even think about the things that were tiresome and bad. Extending your life based on the good aspects is the essence of moral living. 

Then, can the standard of what is good be only what you like? It must be a standard that the nation likes, that the world likes, and that heaven and earth can like. There is certainly a standard that heaven and earth can both like in this universe. If God exists, you must have a relationship with God. Because God is fair, He allows many humans to equally have that standard. 

When will that time be in your life journey? You must strive to rise up, not to go down, centered on that time. In that process, have you become someone who can boast before heaven and earth? In heaven and earth, heaven (天) came first, and then earth (地) came, so if there is a connection, it will align at some point. doesn't matter. If you were to buy a diamond ring worth 700,000 won per carat for women, they would take great care of it day and night, fearing it might get damaged. In the grand scheme, the purpose is precious, while in the smaller scheme, you are precious.

Similarly, as you walk the path of purpose in the future, there may be various forms, but do not boast. Do you think you are wonderful? History and circumstances have led me to this position now, but in my world, I will not lose to anyone.

When you look at it, doesn't the teacher's position seem good? This position may seem good, but the teacher's position is a dangerous one. It is a place where one cannot relax for even a moment. What kind of person is a patriot in a country? It is not someone who eats well and holds a commanding position. It is someone who, while living in rags and eating barley rice in a salt soup, fears that passing foreigners might see their barley rice table, thinking of the country's dignity and trying to hide their appearance. One should not act with jealousy and without dignity, disregarding the dignity and face of their own country. Even if they are in such a position, a patriot is someone who can say that there is no one like them in the country and strives to make their country more beautiful and valuable. When such a person dies, their descendants also become patriots, and patriots are born into that family.

Among us Unification Church members, there are all kinds of people. I still remember a certain young lady. She graduated from university and went out to the countryside for outreach activities. While doing activities, she faced unspeakable persecution. For one year, two years, three years, the persecution continued, and her life was indescribably miserable. During her school days, she had high dreams and had nothing to envy in the world. She had talent, intelligence, and a good family background. However, after entering the door of unification, everything she encountered was nothing but misery. As time passed, the external environment and the difficulties of life began to overwhelm her, and she started to long for the world she had once mocked.

The pitiful situation of a hungry person cannot be understood unless one has experienced hunger. That young lady shed tears, empathizing with the plight of the hungry. Furthermore, when she became so hungry that she longed for rice, she began to criticize her past self, who had once laughed at those who were hungry. She experienced what she had deemed worthless and learned to criticize her past self, but she could not overcome that environment and began to get caught up in it. Even though she vowed to eat barley rice for the purpose, her hands would already reach for the white rice.

The more you enter a difficult position, the more you must grit your teeth and resolve to focus on the purpose. Even if it is a place where death intersects with the cross, you must shed blood and sweat, forget all consciousness of your existence, and make a resolution.

The reason for suffering

When Jesus prayed, "Abba Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will," during his final three prayers, you must understand that when he spoke of the Father's will, he poured out all the strength and energy that did not exist in the world. When he said, "Let it be according to your will," it was not a simple statement. That is why he could not avoid shedding blood and sweat. He pleaded with a strength that did not exist in the world and made a resolution that did not exist in the world.

So, will you suffer for the purpose for three years, or will you suffer for ten years? If you want to leave a true life, what should you do? Which is more true? "It is to suffer for ten years." Will you suffer for ten years or for a hundred years? Between ten years and a hundred years, which suffering is more true? "It is to suffer for a hundred years." Then, will your suffering end with your own life, or will you make your descendants suffer for dozens or even hundreds of generations? What is the true way? If there is someone who says they will only make the Unification Church suffer, and someone who says they will mobilize all 30 million people of the Republic of Korea to suffer, which person is the true patriot? The one who says they will make all 30 million suffer becomes the patriot of that country. If there is someone who says they will mobilize not just 30 million but all of humanity to suffer, that person becomes the world's saint and martyr.

That is why the teachings of the saints have never been about living well and eating well in this world. They teach that even if one lives in poverty, they should help others and live with virtue. Why is that? It is to graft the true. To graft the true, one must do so.

Then, many people think that the teacher only needs to make us suffer for a year, and what is three years of suffering? (Laughter) Although we are not enemies, when thinking about the connection that wants to make things go well, even if it is not three years but ten years of suffering, you must understand that it is the path to receiving blessings.

Choi Joo-chan! Where is Choi Joo-chan? Where is the head of the business department? "I am here." When told to suffer more, they said, "I don't want to. I don't want to." Was that good or bad? (Laughter) Working under the teacher with a position is more meaningful than doing it among yourselves. However, some people feel that what the teacher has entrusted to them is smaller than the title they have among themselves, and they wish the teacher would forget it. Is that a good thought? If you think like that, you will fail.

The teacher has suffered for the purpose until now and is still walking that path, day and night. Those who have not been close to the teacher do not truly know the teacher. The teacher prays on his face as soon as he wakes up. Why does he live like that? Because even in the middle of the night, the beloved children scattered around the world are praying for him and relying on him for God. Even if I cannot put in sincerity, I must at least match the rhythm, right? When the teacher sleeps, he does not know, so God forgives him. During that time, if a child is tired and sleeps, it is like a father watching over them, and God prays in their place.

The teacher does not owe you anything emotionally. Even if it is exhausting, he does not show signs of exhaustion before God. If he sleeps at midnight, he usually wakes up three or four times. He has continued this lifestyle until now. Therefore, even the mother who is close to the teacher cannot help but pray.

When you live in a high place, you always become tired and suffer from nervous breakdowns. Therefore, you must go through a place where you can feel at ease even if a typhoon blows in or a thief comes in. You must enter the valley of the heart and polish yourself from that valley. For that, deep prayer is necessary. You need time to cut off contact with everyone and immerse yourself in deep meditation.

Can you be someone the teacher can trust?

When you look at the teacher now, does he look like someone who has suffered? No matter how angry he may have been, once that moment passes, he does not show it. Because if he makes a mistake, it can cause great harm. He has always been cautious in his life because he should not cause great damage to the purpose because of one person.

That is why, no matter what trials come, he has never resented them. The teacher has been dragged to prison many times until now. He has gone in and out of prison six times without any crime. He has spent four years in prison. The teacher has many stories. However, he has never tried to avoid it or regretted it. Even in the place of torture, he endured, shouting in his heart to hit him more. Many saints have left this world, lamenting and drinking the bitter cup of defeat, but should I be like that? No, I cannot. Hit me! Even if my body bursts from the beating, hit me! At this moment, I am receiving good education from you. Evil has raised a whip against good, but there will come a time when good will raise a whip threefold, sevenfold, or more in retribution. This moment is the time to receive the education that cannot be avoided. So, hit me.

That is how he made his resolution.

Many people have fallen away from believing in the Unification Church until now. There have been all kinds of people gathered before the teacher. There are many people who remain unforgettable in my mind. Sometimes, when I look back from the days in Pyongyang to now, I realize that the various types of people I dealt with in the past are still present here today. Countless human figures have passed by. That is painful. If he trusts you 100% and you turn away, he must bear the cross as much as 100%. That means the person who introduced God will be ashamed because they could only introduce Him that way. Isn’t that the case in the world? That is why there are many hardships regarding how much he should trust you.

Among the various people who followed the teacher in the past, there were those who would even go up to Baekdu Mountain and make a field by breaking the rock there, planting potatoes, and serving the teacher while holding onto a thousand years of resentment.
There was a person who said they would not change even if everything else did. Do you understand what that means? Even if they had to grind a rock and plant a seed there, living with a thousand years of resentment, they swore to live for the will of heaven and to serve their teacher. Everyone, have you heard many stories about Peter? He swore, "Even if everyone else forsakes you, I will never forsake you." (Matthew 26:33) But he denied Jesus three times before the rooster crowed. 

So, will you die for your teacher, or will you live for yourselves? "I will die." Without doing that, even if you say you will die for your teacher, you cannot truly die for him. You must first die for yourselves, and only after being resurrected can you say you will die for your teacher. Those who cannot even die for themselves cannot die for God.

Why must you die? It is for yourselves. You must die to be resurrected. You must die to be reborn. You need to understand this tremendous truth.

You must realize that you have only one life of 70 or 80 years. No matter how long the journey of labor in our lives may be, compared to eternity, it is just a moment that does not even equate to the time it takes to take a single breath. Isn't that right? But how long is eternity? 

Until the sun sets and the moon rises, eternity is at stake. Isn't that so? (Laughter) It is long enough to be that way.

You must have this mindset. 

Just as you grit your teeth and overcome the moment when you are beaten, while you are in this world, you must grit your teeth and move forward for the sake of your purpose. It may seem long, but it is just a moment.

Think about it. If you establish a connection during difficult times, when joy comes, you will not need to be told to establish it. Ordinary people try to establish connections when they are happy. Such connections end up being momentary.

You must be able to stand in a position where you can say, "I will die," even when faced with the life and death of one another. Those who have shared the path of death and endured difficulties together do not even need to think about establishing connections when joy comes. The connections made in difficult times and those made in joyful times have different flavors.

So what is the Unification Church's way? It is to become a person close to God during difficult times. God is suffering because of me, my family, my country, and the world. Therefore, I too must suffer for my personal sake, for my family, for society, for my country, and for the world.

God, there is no one but me. I was born to do this work, so where else could I be? When God has difficulties, please call me. Day or night, do not hesitate to call me. I will follow you anywhere. This is how it should be. Even if no one steps forward, whenever God calls, I will be the one to respond, saying, "Yes, yes," and willingly step forward. Then let’s see whether that person fails or not. That person will never fail.

So, who will the Unification Church suffer with? It is to suffer alongside God, centered on the Republic of Korea. That is the teacher's will and God's will. Then what will you do?

If everyone is suffering, and you are the one who says, "I don't have to do it; someone else will," then you are someone who would sell God. In short, you lack conviction.

Become a pioneer of the path of suffering and leave behind a true life. To walk this path, you must be foolish. Loyal believers are, in some ways, foolish people. They may seem a bit slow-witted. They have a bear-like nature. Even if their arm is cut off, they might say, "Oh, you didn’t cut enough. Cut more." (Laughter) They must have that kind of foolishness. Bears or wild boars, when they are shot and have something hindering them, will bite off that part with their mouths and run away. They think about death later and first cut off what is hindering them. Such foolishness is necessary. Loyal believers must be foolish. Do you understand? They must be a little foolish.

Isn't someone like Stephen seen as a fool in the eyes of the world? A young man not even 30 years old, why would he pray while being stoned, "Forgive them their sins, Lord"? "Yes." Where will you bear the lonely cross? The one who humbly bears it in a joyful place is the faithful person.

Centered around this principle, you must devote yourselves to the economic field, evangelism, and whatever you study, and when you read a page of a book, you must read it with the heart of doing it for God. The Path of Life Due to the Fall
Today, the path of life we are living is not a smooth one. That is why it is reasonable to refer to the course of life as a path of suffering. The rough hills that the families of Adam and Noah had to overcome
We must recognize that God has traversed the rough hills that are difficult to cross because of humanity's fall. If God had not been able to cross those hills, terms like the providence of salvation or restoration would not apply to us today. However, even if God is in a position where He cannot sever the connected environment related to humanity, crossing that connected environment, even if it is the roughest of paths, is possible because God has a clear standard to overcome this. Therefore, we must understand that there remains a day in human history when we can meet God again.

Humanity has fallen into a position unrelated to God due to the fall. Here, humanity has become isolated from God, and the path to seek God has become increasingly distant. When this happens, it is not God who leads, and since humanity has severed its relationship with God, it is humanity itself that must take responsibility. For this reason, even if God sacrifices everything for us, we must go if He commands us to forge ahead. Of course, God has supported the path we must take from behind, but in that journey, humanity has repeatedly left behind the sorrow that has been added to God.

From the perspective of the family of Adam, it was God's will to restore the fall through Cain and Abel because Adam fell. To restore this, Cain had to bring his younger brother Abel as his offering. This hill was a difficult path for Cain to cross. Today, from the perspective of human ethics and morality, it is the most challenging path to cross. However, despite Cain needing to bring Abel with him, he could not cross this rough hill, which means that history must not only return but also face the sorrowful path of the past again.

The rough path to be taken
Because Cain could not cross the rough path he needed to, the history of restoration through humanity has extended from Adam to Noah, ten generations later. Grandfather Noah had to cross another rough hill on behalf of humanity, which was even rougher than the one Cain faced. In Noah's family, the entire family had to cross this rough hill. Therefore, it was not only the father and mother who would go over that hill, but also the children, as members of the family, must unite and overcome the path, even if it involves trials or sufferings of the family, as there is a heavenly mission and a human mission that must be fulfilled.

However, because Noah's family could not cross the rough hill they needed to, God's will, which was centered on the family of Adam, was disrupted. Thus, it became necessary to resolve this matter again through Noah's descendants, which is why, after Noah, there was a period of 400 years of hardship until Abraham was established. Therefore, we understand that God could not help but restart the historical process of trying to cross the rough path.

The rough hill that Abraham had to cross
Now, looking at Abraham, the path he took was not a smooth one. If God could have welcomed and recognized all the connections in the environment he was in when He wanted to relate to him, how wonderful would that have been? However, knowing that such a position would not allow for a connection, God had no choice but to command him to sever all ties. Thus, God commanded Abraham to leave everything behind in his homeland of Ur of the Chaldeans, where his relatives and father lived, and to embark on a path of living as a stranger. God also knew that this was difficult. Although Abraham himself may not have reached the standard known to God, he had an inner faith that he must go through such a time, which is why he received the command and left Ur of the Chaldeans to live as a nomad. This was an indescribably rough path for Abraham.

If Abraham had lamented over the past connections and mourned the ties he left behind while facing the rough hill, the name of Abraham, the first ancestor of faith, would not have remained on this earth today. The path that Abraham took was not a smooth one; a rough hill blocked his way. From this, we can glimpse the fact that one cannot seek heaven without crossing the rough hill.

Where do all these motivations and origins arise? They do not arise from Abraham himself. Because of Abraham, such a path emerged, and if it was his fate to walk that rough path, then the more he was provoked by his own mistakes, the more resolute he would have to be to cross the rough path. However, from Abraham's perspective, there was no reason to cross such a rough hill. Abraham, who was called by God without any historical sins or past mistakes, became the first ancestor of faith.

For Abraham, even though he should have taken a smooth path, he found himself in a position where he had to take a rough hill path, which must have been an indescribable trial for him. However, since Abraham was born as a descendant who could not escape all the connections of his ancestors, he had to cross the rough hill that his ancestors had left behind to return to heaven. Because one cannot return to heaven without stepping on and crossing this hill, God repeatedly commanded him to cross this hill with such content.

To cross this hill according to God's command, Abraham had to forsake his beloved parents and his beloved brother. He also had to completely erase all the possessions he had up to that point, as well as all the connections and concepts he had left behind in that land. Therefore, he could not see a new beginning without stepping over that environment with new connections, that is, new parents and new siblings, with a new heart and new ideals. For this reason, we must understand that God presented Abraham with a difficult hill that no human could cross.

If Abraham had not left everything behind and departed toward the wilderness, which was like a wasteland, we would not have been able to experience a moment of the providence of restoration today. However, because Abraham could smoothly cross that difficult and rough path, we must recognize that a new historical origin was established from there.

Jacob crossing the rough hill
God's command to offer Isaac as a burnt offering was also a rough hill for Abraham. From the perspective of Jacob, fighting with Esau was a rough hill. Because the family of Adam left behind grievances toward God, Jacob, who had to restore the family of Adam, had to go on a fateful path to subdue his older brother Esau to atone for everything that his ancestors, such as Abraham and Isaac, had left behind. This was an extremely difficult task for Jacob. It was also extremely difficult for Esau to submit to his younger brother Jacob. In other words, it was a rough path for both Jacob and Esau.

In the history of restoration, the question of how to cross such rough hills has been at stake. The same goes for Jacob. For Jacob, the 21 years spent in the wilderness was an unbearable path of trial and an unbearable rough path. However, even though Jacob was in a position where the rough path lay before him, he had the faith to step over that rough path with a heart longing for heaven, and even when faced with an environment that rejected all his efforts, he had the conviction to push through, which became a motivation for him to cross the boundary between Haran and Israel.

Because Jacob had such a fervent heart, even when trials and all rough circumstances came upon him, he could overcome them smoothly. Even when evil waves or the schemes of Satan surged according to time and environment, he could overcome them smoothly. He had a foundation of conviction that allowed him to push through without being dominated or invaded from the inside or outside. Jacob believed that those days of trial were a training ground that would lead him to find his family and, further, to attain the desired Israel, which is why he could overcome those days of trial.

If he had not been able to overcome those days of trial, he would not have been able to appear with the status of the chosen people of Israel. It took Jacob 21 long years to find that status. The path he traversed over those 21 years was a path of grievance, a path of trial, and a rough path, but because Jacob pursued heaven, seeking Israel without caring about such a path, we must recognize that the history of the chosen people began from there.

From this perspective, Jacob was not a cunning person. In his life, he experienced sorrows that no one else had encountered in the historical process. Because he was more determined than anyone else to return to heaven, he was able to overcome and break through the difficult hills he faced in his environment. Therefore, we must understand that he was able to cross the steep mountains and ridges that lay in his way for 21 years.

From the day the Israelite nation started on the side of heaven, they inherited Jacob's faith and continued to serve the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob, or through the connections of family tradition, they had to live their lives solely for God. However, because the Israelite nation could not do this, the rough hills that the Israelite nation had to overcome in the historical process, or the rough hills that Jacob had crossed, came back to confront their descendants.

Thus, before the family that has crossed the family hill lies the tribal hill, and before the Israelite nation that has crossed the national hill lies the national hill, and before the Israelite nation that has crossed the national hill lies the world hill. We must recognize that there are even larger and rougher hills remaining on the path of restoration.

Connecting this historical narrative, God has given the Israelite nation the mission to cross a great mountain range that leads to the foundation of a nation and to the stage of the world, raising the banner of liberation for all people to establish a new heaven and earth on this land. This is why God has given the Israelite nation the thought of the Messiah to create a new world. We must understand that until now has been a period of preparation to cross that hill.

The Workers of New Cultural Creation

Among the young ones, there are bad ones who do evil deeds, but there are also useful ones. Just like the tree of the knowledge of good and evil, there are those who can become evil and those who can become good. 

If a young man jumps onto the platform and shouts to the crowd, stirring their hearts like ripples in a calm lake, igniting hope for tomorrow, then indeed, he is a valuable young man! Isn't that right? 

The reason the teacher calls you young ones is because it means you did well, so you should interpret it correctly. The term "young one" is closer to the teacher than "young person." Young people are difficult to handle. However, young ones are easier to manage. Do you prefer something easy to handle or something difficult? "Easy is better." Easy is good. So, "young one!" 

October 3, 1969 (Friday), Donggureung.

(Laughter) That's how the teacher interprets it.

In that position, no one in the Republic of Korea is envious. Why do they listen to the teacher's words so well? Because they find joy in doing so. 

The difference in marriage concepts between Eastern and Western people

This time, there was something interesting about the marriages. I was going to talk about it, but there are only three minutes left, so let's save that for later. Shall we move to Act 2? "No." Then are you saying you want to run back? "Yes." If women break their legs while running, don’t blame the teacher. If they become crippled and cannot get married or go to university to become a bachelor, let alone a doctor, they might think, "Oh, the fate of a Unification Church member is hard." Wouldn't that be so? If they break their legs, they might say, "Oh, I ruined my fate!" (Laughter) How do you feel, everyone? Is that right? Women? Wouldn't that be so? If you are running, those with pumpkin-shaped bodies run well. If they break their legs while running, would they blame the teacher? "No." You looked down when you answered; I was asking you. Women should say they walked so that they will be loved by their husbands later. 

Koreans, Germans, Japanese, Americans, and people from dozens of countries have been directly married by the teacher. However, when Korean people encounter their marriage partners, they may not speak actively, but they calculate everything about whether the other person is good or bad.
