At such times, how astonishing it must be for the teacher! When the teacher asks and sees how they respond, some people stand silently for over an hour without saying anything. 

However, Western people are different. They need explanations first when it comes to marriage. The teacher explains that it is better for older women to marry younger men. Then they listen well to the teacher. But it is very difficult for Eastern people like those from Japan or Korea. The Eastern concept is that the bride should be younger. This is a traditional custom. However, Western people are the opposite. In the future, it is best for marriages to be between extremes. (Laughter) Why is that? Is it because they like it or because they dislike it? 

Now, if I were to go into detail about that, it would never end, so I will only mention a special incident. In America, there is now a Samba class. This is a gathering of women who deserve recognition for pioneering our church in America. How old are they? They are all around 42 or 43 years old. If they were married, they would all have children. We must bless these people, but finding a partner for them has been a big problem since the teacher arrived here. 

So when the teacher went there and explained that problem, they understood it well. It is clear that Western people have transcended such concepts. A 42-year-old woman is like an aunt, yet a 33-year-old young man wants to marry her. There is a nine-year age difference between 33 and 42. 

The British family was also all in America. A 42-year-old person and a 33-year-old person should marry, but is there anyone who thinks that is not okay? Think about whether you can do it. Think quietly. (Laughter) Consider how old your aunt or uncle is. They would be at the age to have two or three children, so their faces might be wrinkled and lacking in color. Imagine marrying a woman who looks like that aunt instead of a flower-like young person. How does that feel? Does it feel good or not? Speak honestly, men? "Not good." That's right. The answer that it does not feel good is the principle. 

Then did the teacher force them to marry? No, that’s not it. What they see is not just age. They highly respect honor. They consider how much achievement and merit a person has, which represents that person's character. Achievements and merits represent the whole person. That concept is different from that of Eastern people. Why is that? Because they value living well for a short time more than living long. In that sense, I felt that they have a progressive aspect. 

The life and thoughts of the Dutch missionary

It was not just one person who felt this way. There was also a person named Teddy among those who pioneered in the Netherlands. He was a well-known technician who graduated from a considerable technical school in America. When he met the teacher, he went to the Netherlands to evangelize, pioneering the Dutch church and becoming a significant ancestor there. Listening to him, one can understand that he had many hardships. He was a person who vowed to spend more than three months in the Netherlands for the indemnity period. He gave up everything and worked as a dockworker at the wharf. He was a competent technician who earned about $1,300 a month in America, and even with just a certificate, he could receive great treatment anywhere in the Netherlands, yet he threw it all away and became a dockworker at the wharf. 

When the teacher visited, he was living with the sailors. The situation was quite difficult. His hands were like those of a toad, and his face looked like that of a laborer. He was completely worn out. At mealtime, he ate hard bread. He could only earn $38 a day. Despite being busy making a living, he managed to save some money to translate and publish the principles. He even wrote a blood letter in that book and presented it to the teacher. Seeing that, the teacher felt deeply moved. 

When he was going around evangelizing, he walked everywhere, so the teacher asked if he wanted a motorcycle, but he said he didn't like motorcycles. When the teacher asked what he wanted, he said he wanted a bicycle. So the teacher bought him one. The bicycle was bought four years ago, and he thought that even if the president or anyone else touched it, it would be a big deal, so he has not ridden it until now, and it remains as new. He is a person who has devoted himself this much. 

This time, when it came to blessing, the teacher could not overlook the people of Europe. So he gathered all the candidates and asked the leaders to prepare a list in advance. While others had partners they hoped for, this person had no one in mind. When asked who he wanted to be blessed with, he said he knew someone who had truly been loyal and followed the path while he was in America. When asked who that was, he said it was a woman named Pauline. She was a member who joined at the age of 33 and had been a member for eight years, forming a trinity with another member named Doris. She was one of the three revolutionary fighters for our cause. 

When he walked the path with her in America, he accumulated...
There seem to have been many contributions, but it appears there were also many happy times. Furthermore, he, who pioneered Holland, knows well that she has been living a pioneering life alone for over ten years, no matter how difficult the circumstances. Upon hearing that she has not yet married, the teacher had inquired whether he could marry her while he was in Germany. 

There are many beauties in the world, and there are many young women in the Holland church, but a woman without experience in social life cannot become a wife who can embrace the Holland church in the future. Of course, there are many pretty and hardworking young ladies in the Holland church, but that is not the issue. In order to leave the tradition of the Unification Church in Holland, a mother-like person who loves Holland and can bear all the hardships inside and out is needed. Therefore, he expressed a desire for a blessing with that lady-like woman who is currently in America, regardless of what others might think. 

So, I said, "Hey, you! That lady-like woman looks like a horse!" and described her as someone who seems to walk around with her words. How would you feel if you heard such words? Good or bad? 

When the person who was told to gather those who did not receive blessings met that lady-like woman, he was shocked and exclaimed, "What kind of woman is this?" He remarked that if she were that unattractive, she would truly be unattractive. With a long face, if her forehead is exposed, it looks unappealing; her back is hunched, her nose is big, and her height is such that even a wrestling player would be overshadowed. If an ordinary man saw her smile, he would probably pack his bags in surprise and run away. Yet, despite all this, that man says he wants to live with her for a hundred years. 

Seeing this, would the teacher have felt good or bad? "He would have felt good." Initially, he felt bad. Why? Because the teacher wanted to give a beautiful young lady to the young man. He hoped for a better future, someone who would bloom like the most beautiful flower and emit the sweetest fragrance, someone he could love day and night. However, since this was already far from his expectations, he felt bad. But what made him feel good? It was the intention to establish a strong foundation for the sake of God’s people and the three million citizens of Holland. Furthermore, he said that in order to do such things, men must become those who can elevate the authority of women. The teacher raised his hand to his words. 

On the day of the wedding, the teacher thoroughly made him promise. An older woman, after a little while, would face issues with childbirth. Since she is now forty-two years old, there are only four years left in which she can give birth. However, he said that it was possible to have children. He stated that it was not a problem. God loves us more than anyone else and will create the most blessed family among European families. Wouldn't the Creator, God, give us children to fulfill the expectations of a son-in-law? With that, he surpasses much older men. 

I asked Teddy again whether he would really send someone to evangelize to be his wife or not. He responded, "Do you not trust me?" and seemed to feel bad. Europe has such people, and thus authority is established. 

Once on a plane, one can quickly fly to America. So she came right away. I appreciated her from the perspective of that man. 

"Oh! Because the woman looks like that..." and the teacher also became interested. Young ladies worry about where they might end up when sent for pioneering evangelism, but such a woman could go alone to the Arctic region for a thousand years without any worries. Furthermore, she has a lot of social experience, so she is not lacking as a mother both at home and in the church. And knowing that she is older, she understands that humility must be her life philosophy to attract a younger husband. She knows that she must not be without humility. 

To embrace Westerners, if you look at American women, how big are their figures? Such women walk around almost exposing their large chests. When I went in front of the White House, I saw women barely covering important parts, and the teacher felt very bad about it. Seeing that they do not even realize it is shameful, I think they have quite a bit of nerve. I fear what would happen if someone were to wink at or hug such a woman. 

When entering hotel restaurants, men must wear ties and formal attire even in the middle of summer, but women can boldly enter without such requirements. What kind of country is this? Seeing this makes me feel very bad. Women feel good about it, right? That is why women are indeed good, but as time goes on, the number of women living alone is increasing. In that country, while women are served, they are also looked down upon. That is why American women are all disliked. 

This is because American people have traveled abroad. They have been to the Soviet Union, Japan, and Europe, and when comparing women in the Western civilization sphere with those in the Asian civilization sphere, they realize that Eastern women are much better. That is why more men are living single, and issues like homosexuality are becoming problematic in Congress. Thus, the number of women living alone is increasing. 

When a woman who has lived like that meets a man, based on the principle of relativity, who is the subject? Is the subject of the heart the woman and the subject of the body the man? Is that so? How about it? Are both subjects? Is the man the subject or is the woman the subject? Who has more affection? Women have more affection than men. In that sense, women are the subjects. However, no matter how much affection there is, for that affection to become true affection, they must meet and serve a man. Is that not so? The field of affection is the woman, and the seed of affection is the man. There is a field because there is a seed, not the other way around. When centered on the seed, the field is the object. 

From that perspective, looking at the letters that have come recently, it seems that to become equal men and women, they are working very hard, and the church is experiencing considerable revival. When I see this, I realize that the awareness of public consciousness is much more advanced in Westerners than in Easterners. Do you think about public matters? You are only thinking about your own benefit right now. You must understand that you cannot follow the Europeans in the future. Since we must also embrace the Europeans, we must possess a higher morality. 

You must be able to say, "I am superior to you." Will you do that? "Yes." 

In the future, young men must have the generosity to marry women who are more than ten years older than them to surpass the teacher. Do you feel good about that? (Laughter) Why? Do you not feel good? Even if she is the only princess in that country, do you not feel good? Even if she is the only woman in that country, do you not feel good? What will you do if there is only one woman? What if the ratio of men to women is 1000 to 1? Will you feel empowered or not? 

Those who have worked for America will remain in American history. When I look at the women who have worked with this intention, I do not know how they feel, but the inherent origin that can brilliantly illuminate history arises from them. That is why it is easy for the teacher to talk to them. As soon as he opens his mouth, they already catch on. So, he can easily explain everything. However, you all feel bad about even small matters. They do not show any signs even if they slightly frown their big eyes. But Eastern people have small eyes, so even a slight frown shows immediately. Westerners have such big eyes that even a slight frown does not give any clue. But you all show it immediately even with a slight frown. 

Regarding the view on marriage that Unification Church members should have, it seems that Westerners are significantly ahead of Easterners. Therefore, we must learn from them regarding the view of marriage. We must learn, right? We must learn. When looking at the restoration process, would the teacher not have such thoughts? 

If God were to designate the king of kings among the black people on the foundation where He has worked for 6,000 years, what would the teacher do? When the teacher first embarked on this path, he had such thoughts. Would he sincerely welcome him? Could he truly, truly welcome him? What do you think? You must understand that you cannot rise from there. 

Do not think of becoming the husband of a beauty when marrying. You should think of becoming the husband of an ordinary woman and live better than anyone else. Thus, you must become a husband who can admire any beauty in the world. Do you understand what I mean? You must have that perspective to treat women well. 

Why am I telling you all this? Right now, some people are well-built and capable, and they are considered useful people in our Unification world, but there are concerns about them as well. They decide their lives centered around themselves. Those who think centered on themselves are doomed. Is that not so? If a person who thinks centered on themselves marries a wife who thinks centered on herself, both will fall together. Is that not so? Then what must be done to avoid falling? You must have the ability to digest marriage and a substantial foundation that can surpass it centered on the intention. Without this, you will surely fail. That is inevitable. Then who will do that for you? The teacher will do it. That is why the teacher has been giving blessings until now. 

To ensure a harmonious family, when the teacher gives blessings, extremes must meet. You must not let the east meet the east or the north meet the north. The north and south, east and west must meet. Should you give a tall man a tall woman or a short woman? A fat man does not like a fat woman. Also, a fat woman does not like a fat man. Would a slender man like a fat woman or a slender woman? Think about it. Who would he like? He would like a fat woman, right? "Yes." If he does not like a fat woman and he is also slender, what will happen if the woman is also slender? If there are only big trees on the mountain, it is not pleasant to look at. There should also be small trees. 

When the teacher has been giving blessings, he has surely said that this pair will have a dozen children, and it will definitely come true. (Laughter) What I think now is the same. When the teacher marries people, he does not do it carelessly. Because the teacher pairs dozens of couples in one evening, people in the world think it is done carelessly. However, what the teacher says is certain. Therefore, those who read fortunes, face readings, and compatibility reports say that those pairs are the best. If you do not believe it, go directly to those who read fortunes, face readings, and compatibility reports and ask them. It will surely match perfectly. 

Even though the teacher pairs dozens of couples in a day, they all say that their fortunes, face readings, and compatibility reports are the best. If they were to do it, they would have to spend all day carefully to pair one couple, but the teacher can do dozens in a day, and the fortune tellers admire it and promote our Unification Church. They are doing a good job of promoting our Unification Church. Thus, the history that will control the fortunes of the world will unfold in an instant centered around the fundamental issues of life. Therefore, in the future, blessed families must become one. 

Seeing this, you must establish the ideal of heaven centered around the family in the future. Therefore, you must think deeply about the family. Do you understand? You must become the prince of the family. In terms of history, you must also become the prince of the subject. To do this, you must have the integrity of a man. You must do this with the integrity of a man. 

Until now, I have emphasized the integrity of women, right? Who lost integrity in the Garden of Eden? Did the woman lose it, or did the man lose it? "The woman." Is that so? The man also lost it. The man, who is the center of Eden, also lost it. Adam was entangled with Eve and eventually cut off even the original root, the man. It was Eve, the woman, who caused the fall of Adam, the man. Because of that, women have been violated by men until now. Is that not so? The reason women are violated by men is because of that. That is why the teacher is conducting the movement for gender equality and women's liberation. It must be done for future generations more than for anyone in the world. Men have become displeased because of women. When looking at women and men, strangely, men seem to be more displeased. That is the position. 

Now, to fulfill your intentions, even if you marry an American woman, you must be able to rejoice. You must not only think of yourself. If that woman has the right conditions, you must shout "Hooray!" Do you have the confidence to shout "Hooray"? (The rest is not recorded) *
